           How to Clean Up and Expand a Garden
          </a>
         </h2>
         <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
          Want to learn how to take an overgrown flower bed and transform it into a beautiful garden? Watch as Landscape Contractor Jenn Nawada cleans up the garden by pruning, dividing, and defining the edges.

              <h3 class="c-entry-box-base__headline">
               <a data-analytics-link="sitegroup" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.thisoldhouse.com/this-old-house">
                This Old House
               </a>
              </h3>
              <p class="c-entry-box-base__dek p-dek c-entry-box-base__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="group_description">
               This Old House restores a fire-damaged 1905 three-family home in Dorchester, MA. Episodes air the first week of April on PBS. Check your local listings.
              </p>

   var phonographEvents = phonographEvents || [];
      (function() {
        var continent = document.cookie.match(/_chorus_geoip_continent=([^;]+)/i) || [];
        var data = { 'Page Title':document.title, 'GA Track Prefix':'t1.', 'geoip_continent': continent[1] };
        var dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
        dataLayer
          .filter(function(m) { return !!m['Network'] })
          .forEach(function(m) {
            Object.keys(m).forEach(function(k) { data[k] = m[k] });
          });

        var userid = data['Logged in Status'];
        data['User ID'] = (typeof userid === 'number') ? userid : null;
        phonographEvents.push(['pageload', data]);
      })();
  </script>
